      <p>
       <b>
        Andorra
       </b>
       (
       <span class="nowrap">
        <span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt">
         <a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">
          /
          <span style="border-bottom:1px dotted">
           <span title="/æ/: 'a' in 'bad'">
            æ
           </span>
           <span title="'n' in 'nigh'">
            n
           </span>
           <span title="/ˈ/: primary stress follows">
            ˈ
           </span>
           <span title="'d' in 'dye'">
            d
           </span>
           <span title="/ɔːr/: 'ar' in 'war'">
            ɔːr
           </span>
           <span title="/ə/: 'a' in 'about'">
            ə
           </span>
          </span>
          /
         </a>
        </span>
        <small class="nowrap">
         (
         <span class="unicode haudio">
          <span class="fn">
           <span style="white-space:nowrap">
            <a href="/wiki/File:En-us-Andorra.ogg" title="About this sound">
             <img alt="About this sound" data-file-height="20" data-file-width="20" height="11" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/11px-Loudspeaker.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/17px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/22px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 2x" width="11"/>
            </a>
           </span>
           <a class="internal" href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3e/En-us-Andorra.ogg" title="En-us-Andorra.ogg">
            listen
           </a>
          </span>
         </span>
         )
        </small>
       </span>
       ;
       <small>
        Catalan:
       </small>
       <span class="IPA" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">
        <a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Catalan" title="Help:IPA/Catalan">
         [ənˈdorə]
        </a>
       </span>
       ,
       <small>
        locally
       </small>
       <span class="IPA" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">
        <a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Catalan" title="Help:IPA/Catalan">
         [anˈdɔra]
        </a>
       </span>
       ), officially the
       <b>
        Principality of Andorra
       </b>
       (
       <a href="/wiki/Catalan_language" title="Catalan language">
        Catalan
       </a>
       :
       <i>
        <span lang="ca">
         Principat d'Andorra
        </span>
       </i>
       ), also called the
       <b>
        Principality of the Valleys of Andorra
       </b>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6">
        <a href="#cite_note-6">
         [6]
        </a>
       </sup>
       (Catalan:
       <i>
        <span lang="ca">
         Principat de les Valls d'Andorra
        </span>
       </i>
       ), is a
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sovereign" title="Sovereign">
        sovereign
       </a>
       landlocked
       <a href="/wiki/Microstate" title="Microstate">
        microstate
       </a>
       in
       <a href="/wiki/Iberian_Peninsula" title="Iberian Peninsula">
        Southwestern Europe
       </a>
       , located in the eastern
       <a href="/wiki/Pyrenees" title="Pyrenees">
        Pyrenees
       </a>
       mountains and bordered by
       <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">
        France
       </a>
       in the north, and the
       <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">
        Spanish
       </a>
       autonomous community of
       <a href="/wiki/Catalonia" title="Catalonia">
        Catalonia
       </a>
       in the south. Created under a charter in 988
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify">
          <span title="The text near this tag may need clarification or removal of jargon. (December 2017)">
           clarification needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
       , the present principality
       <a href="/wiki/Par%C3%A9age_of_Andorra_1278" title="Paréage of Andorra 1278">
        was formed
       </a>
       in 1278. It is known as a
       <a href="/wiki/Principality" title="Principality">
        principality
       </a>
       as it is a
       <a href="/wiki/Diarchy" title="Diarchy">
        diarchy
       </a>
       headed by two
       <a href="/wiki/Co-Princes_of_Andorra" title="Co-Princes of Andorra">
        Co-Princes
       </a>
       – the Catholic
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bishop_of_Urgell" title="Bishop of Urgell">
        Bishop of Urgell
       </a>
       in Spain and the
       <a href="/wiki/President_of_France" title="President of France">
        President of France
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       Andorra is the
       <a href="/wiki/European_microstates" title="European microstates">
        sixth-smallest nation in Europe
       </a>
       , having an area of 468 km
       <sup>
        2
       </sup>
       (181 sq mi) and a population of approximately 77,281.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-UN_WPP_2-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-UN_WPP-2">
         [2]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Andorra is the 16th-smallest country in the world by land and 11th-smallest country by population.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7">
        <a href="#cite_note-7">
         [7]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Its capital
       <a href="/wiki/Andorra_la_Vella" title="Andorra la Vella">
        Andorra la Vella
       </a>
       is the highest capital city in Europe, at an elevation of 1,023 metres (3,356 feet)
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Above_mean_sea_level" title="Above mean sea level">
        above sea level
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8">
        <a href="#cite_note-8">
         [8]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The official language is
       <a href="/wiki/Catalan_language" title="Catalan language">
        Catalan
       </a>
       , although Spanish, Portuguese, and French are also commonly spoken.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cia_1-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-cia-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9">
        <a href="#cite_note-9">
         [9]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       <a href="/wiki/Tourism_in_Andorra" title="Tourism in Andorra">
        Andorra's tourism
       </a>
       services an estimated 10.2 million visitors annually.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-es2_10-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-es2-10">
         [10]
        </a>
       </sup>
       It is not a member of the
       <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">
        European Union
       </a>
       , but the
       <a href="/wiki/Euro" title="Euro">
        euro
       </a>
       is the official currency. It has been a member of the
       <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">
        United Nations
       </a>
       since 1993.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11">
        <a href="#cite_note-11">
         [11]
        </a>
       </sup>
       In 2013, the people of Andorra had
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_life_expectancy" title="List of countries by life expectancy">
        the highest life expectancy in the world
       </a>
       at 81 years, according to the
       <a href="/wiki/Global_Burden_of_Disease_Study" title="Global Burden of Disease Study">
        Global Burden of Disease Study
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12">
        <a href="#cite_note-12">
         [12]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
      </p>

       <div class="toctitle" dir="ltr" lang="en">
        <h2>
         Contents
        </h2>
