          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left">
          <b>
           <a href="/wiki/Emmanuel_Macron" title="Emmanuel Macron">
            Emmanuel Macron
           </a>
          </b>
          <br/>
          –  current
          <a href="/wiki/List_of_Co-Princes_of_Andorra" title="List of Co-Princes of Andorra">
           French Co-Prince of Andorra
          </a>
          since 14 May 2017
         </div>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:left">
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Andorra is a parliamentary
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Co-principality" title="Co-principality">
        co-principality
       </a>
       with the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/President_of_the_French_Republic" title="President of the French Republic">
        President of France
       </a>
       and the
       <a href="/wiki/Catholic_Church" title="Catholic Church">
        Catholic
       </a>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bishop_of_Urgell" title="Bishop of Urgell">
        Bishop of Urgell
       </a>
       (
       <a href="/wiki/Catalonia" title="Catalonia">
        Catalonia
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">
        Spain
       </a>
       ) as
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_Co-Princes_of_Andorra" title="List of Co-Princes of Andorra">
        Co-Princes
       </a>
       . This peculiarity makes the President of France, in his capacity as
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Prince_of_Andorra" title="Prince of Andorra">
        Prince of Andorra
       </a>
       , an elected reigning monarch, although he is not elected by a popular vote of the Andorran people. The politics of Andorra take place in a framework of a
       <a href="/wiki/Parliamentary_system" title="Parliamentary system">
        parliamentary
       </a>
       <a href="/wiki/Representative_democracy" title="Representative democracy">
        representative democracy
       </a>
       , whereby the
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_government_of_Andorra" title="List of heads of government of Andorra">
        Head of Government
       </a>
       is the
       <a href="/wiki/Head_of_government" title="Head of government">
        chief executive
       </a>
       , and of a
       <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/pluriform" title="wiktionary:pluriform">
        pluriform
       </a>
       multi-party system.
      </p>
      <p>
       The current Head of Government is
       <a href="/wiki/Antoni_Mart%C3%AD" title="Antoni Martí">
        Antoni Martí
       </a>
       of the
       <a href="/wiki/Democrats_for_Andorra" title="Democrats for Andorra">
        Democrats for Andorra
       </a>
       (DA).
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Executive_power" title="Executive power">
        Executive power
       </a>
       is exercised by the government. Legislative power is vested in both government and parliament.
      </p>
      <p>
       The Parliament of Andorra is known as the General Council. The General Council consists of between 28 and 42 Councillors. The Councillors serve for four-year terms, and elections are held between the 30th and 40th days following the dissolution of the previous Council.
      </p>
      <p>
       Half are elected in equal numbers by each of the seven administrative parishes, and the other half of the Councillors are elected in a single national constituency. Fifteen days after the election, the Councillors hold their inauguration. During this session, the Syndic General, who is the head of the General Council, and the Subsyndic General, his assistant, are elected. Eight days later, the Council convenes once more. During this session the Head of Government is chosen from among the Councillors.
      </p>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Casa_de_la_Vall_-_18.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2222" data-file-width="3560" height="137" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/Casa_de_la_Vall_-_18.jpg/220px-Casa_de_la_Vall_-_18.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/Casa_de_la_Vall_-_18.jpg/330px-Casa_de_la_Vall_-_18.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/Casa_de_la_Vall_-_18.jpg/440px-Casa_de_la_Vall_-_18.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Casa_de_la_Vall_-_18.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Casa de la Vall, Andorran Parliament
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Candidates can be proposed by a minimum of one-fifth of the Councillors. The Council then elects the candidate with the absolute majority of votes to be Head of Government. The Syndic General then notifies the Co-Princes, who in turn appoint the elected candidate as the Head of Government of Andorra. The General Council is also responsible for proposing and passing laws. Bills may be presented to the Council as Private Members' Bills by three of the local Parish Councils jointly or by at least one tenth of the citizens of Andorra.
      </p>
      <p>
       The Council also approves the annual budget of the principality. The government must submit the proposed budget for parliamentary approval at least two months before the previous budget expires. If the budget is not approved by the first day of the next year, the previous budget is extended until a new one is approved. Once any bill is approved, the Syndic General is responsible for presenting it to the Co-Princes so that they may sign and enact it.
      </p>
      <p>
       If the Head of Government is not satisfied with the Council, he may request that the Co-Princes dissolve the Council and order new elections. In turn, the Councillors have the power to remove the Head of Government from office. After a motion of censure is approved by at least one-fifth of the Councillors, the Council will vote and if it receives the absolute majority of votes, the Head of Government is removed.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Law_and_criminal_justice">
        Law and criminal justice
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Andorra&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Law and criminal justice">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       The judiciary is composed of the Magistrates Court, the Criminal Law Court, the High Court of Andorra, and the Constitutional Court. The High Court of Justice is composed of five judges: one appointed by the Head of Government, one each by the Co-Princes, one by the Syndic General, and one by the Judges and Magistrates. It is presided over by the member appointed by the Syndic General and the judges hold office for six-year terms.
      </p>
      <p>
       The Magistrates and Judges are appointed by the High Court, as is the President of the Criminal Law Court. The High Court also appoints members of the Office of the Attorney General. The Constitutional Court is responsible for interpreting the Constitution and reviewing all appeals of unconstitutionality against laws and treaties. It is composed of four judges, one appointed by each of the Co-Princes and two by the General Council. They serve eight-year terms. The Court is presided over by one of the Judges on a two-year rotation so that each judge at one point will preside over the Court.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span id="Foreign_relations.2C_defence.2C_and_security">
       </span>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Foreign_relations,_defence,_and_security">
        Foreign relations, defence, and security
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Andorra&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Foreign relations, defence, and security">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_Andorra" title="Foreign relations of Andorra">
        Foreign relations of Andorra
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bruxelles_rue_de_la_Montagne_10.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3888" data-file-width="2592" height="330" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/Bruxelles_rue_de_la_Montagne_10.jpg/220px-Bruxelles_rue_de_la_Montagne_10.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/Bruxelles_rue_de_la_Montagne_10.jpg/330px-Bruxelles_rue_de_la_Montagne_10.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/Bruxelles_rue_de_la_Montagne_10.jpg/440px-Bruxelles_rue_de_la_Montagne_10.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Bruxelles_rue_de_la_Montagne_10.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         The embassy of Andorra in
         <a href="/wiki/Brussels" title="Brussels">
          Brussels
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Andorra does not have its own armed forces,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cia_1-2">
        <a href="#cite_note-cia-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
       although there is a small ceremonial army. Responsibility for defending the nation rests primarily with
       <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">
        France
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">
        Spain
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-94">
        <a href="#cite_note-94">
         [94]
        </a>
       </sup>
       However, in case of emergencies or natural disasters, the
       <i>
        Sometent
       </i>
       (an alarm) is called and all able-bodied men between 21 and 60 of Andorran nationality must serve.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95">
        <a href="#cite_note-95">
         [95]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-recarrega.net_96-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-recarrega.net-96">
         [96]
        </a>
       </sup>
       This is why all Andorrans, and especially the head of each house (usually the eldest able-bodied man of a house) should, by law, keep a rifle, even though the law also states that the police will offer a firearm in case of need.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-recarrega.net_96-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-recarrega.net-96">
         [96]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Andorra is a full member of the United Nations (UN), the
       <a href="/wiki/Organization_for_Security_and_Co-operation_in_Europe" title="Organization for Security and Co-operation in Europe">
        Organization for Security and Co-operation in Europe
       </a>
       (OSCE), and has a special agreement with the European Union (EU).
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Military">
        Military
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Andorra&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Military">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Andorra has a small army, which has historically been raised or reconstituted at various dates, but has never in modern times amounted to a standing army. The basic principle of Andorran defence is that all able-bodied men are available to fight if called upon by the sounding of the
       <i>
        Sometent
       </i>
       . Being a
       <a href="/wiki/Landlocked_country" title="Landlocked country">
        landlocked country
       </a>
       , Andorra has no
       <a href="/wiki/Navy" title="Navy">
        navy
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       Prior to World War I, Andorra maintained an armed force of about 600 part-time militiamen. This body was not liable for service outside the principality and was commanded by two officials (
       <i>
        viguiers
       </i>
       ) appointed by France and the Bishop of Urgell.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_64-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-64">
         [64]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Despite not being involved in any fighting during the
       <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">
        First World War
       </a>
       , Andorra was technically the longest combatant, as the country was left out of the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Versailles_Peace_Conference" title="Versailles Peace Conference">
        Versailles Peace Conference
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/De_jure" title="De jure">
        technically
       </a>
       remaining at war with Germany from its original declaration of war in 1914 until 24 September 1958 when Andorra officially declared peace with Germany.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-DYKAndorra_87-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-DYKAndorra-87">
         [87]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-97">
        <a href="#cite_note-97">
         [97]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       In the modern era, the army has consisted of a very small body of volunteers willing to undertake ceremonial duties. Uniforms were handed down from generation to generation within families and communities.
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2017)">
           citation needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The army's role in internal security was largely taken over by the formation of the
       <a href="/wiki/Police_Corps_of_Andorra" title="Police Corps of Andorra">
        Police Corps of Andorra
       </a>
       in 1931. Brief civil disorder associated with the elections of 1933 led to assistance being sought from the French
       <a href="/wiki/National_Gendarmerie" title="National Gendarmerie">
        National Gendarmerie
       </a>
       , with a detachment resident in Andorra for two months under the command of René-Jules Baulard.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-98">
        <a href="#cite_note-98">
         [98]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The Andorran Army was reformed in the following year, with eleven soldiers appointed to supervisory roles.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-99">
        <a href="#cite_note-99">
         [99]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The force consisted of six
       <a href="/wiki/Corporal" title="Corporal">
        Corporals
       </a>
       , one for each parish (although there are currently seven parishes, there were only six until 1978), plus four junior staff officers to co-ordinate action, and a commander with the rank of major. It was the responsibility of the six corporals, each in his own parish, to be able to raise a fighting force from among the able-bodied men of the parish.
      </p>
      <p>
       Today a small, twelve-man ceremonial unit remains the only permanent section of the Andorran Army, but all able-bodied men remain technically available for military service,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-100">
        <a href="#cite_note-100">
         [100]
        </a>
       </sup>
       with a requirement for each family to have access to a firearm. The army has not fought for more than 700 years, and its main responsibility is to present the
       <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_Andorra" title="Flag of Andorra">
        flag of Andorra
       </a>
       at official ceremonial functions.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-101">
        <a href="#cite_note-101">
         [101]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-102">
        <a href="#cite_note-102">
         [102]
        </a>
       </sup>
       According to
       <a href="/wiki/Marc_Forn%C3%A9_Moln%C3%A9" title="Marc Forné Molné">
        Marc Forné Molné
       </a>
       , Andorra's military budget is strictly from voluntary donations, and the availability of full-time volunteers.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-103">
        <a href="#cite_note-103">
         [103]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The myth that all members of the Andorran Army are ranked as officers is popularly maintained in many works of reference.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-104">
        <a href="#cite_note-104">
         [104]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-105">
        <a href="#cite_note-105">
         [105]
        </a>
       </sup>
       In reality, all those serving in the permanent ceremonial reserve hold ranks as
       <a href="/wiki/Officer_(armed_forces)" title="Officer (armed forces)">
        officers
       </a>
       , or
       <a href="/wiki/Non-commissioned_officer" title="Non-commissioned officer">
        non-commissioned officers
       </a>
       , because the
       <a href="/wiki/Enlisted_rank" title="Enlisted rank">
        other ranks
       </a>
       are considered to be the rest of the able-bodied male population, who may still be called upon by the
       <i>
        Sometent
       </i>
       to serve, although such a call has not been made in modern times.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Police_Corps">
        Police Corps
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Andorra&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Police Corps">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Police_Corps_of_Andorra" title="Police Corps of Andorra">
        Police Corps of Andorra
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       Andorra maintains a small but modern and well-equipped internal police force, with around 240 police officers supported by civilian assistants. The principal services supplied by the corps are uniformed community policing, criminal detection, border control, and traffic policing. There are also small specialist units including police dogs, mountain rescue, and a bomb disposal team.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-106">
        <a href="#cite_note-106">
         [106]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="GIPA">
        GIPA
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Andorra&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: GIPA">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h4>
      <p>
       The
       <i>
        Grup d'Intervenció Policia d'Andorra
       </i>
       (GIPA) is a small special forces unit trained in
       <a href="/wiki/Counter-terrorism" title="Counter-terrorism">
        counter-terrorism
       </a>
       , and
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hostage_negotiator" title="Hostage negotiator">
        hostage recovery
       </a>
       tasks. Although it is the closest in style to an active military force, it is part of the
       <a href="/wiki/Police_Corps_of_Andorra" title="Police Corps of Andorra">
        Police Corps
       </a>
       , and not the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Military_of_Andorra" title="Military of Andorra">
        army
       </a>
       . As terrorist and hostage situations are a rare threat to the nation, the GIPA is commonly assigned to prisoner escort duties, and at other times to routine policing.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-107">
        <a href="#cite_note-107">
         [107]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Fire_brigade">
        Fire brigade
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Andorra&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Fire brigade">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The
       <i>
        Andorran Fire Brigade
       </i>
       , with headquarters at
       <a href="/wiki/Santa_Coloma_d%27Andorra" title="Santa Coloma d'Andorra">
        Santa Coloma
       </a>
       , operates from four modern fire stations, and has a staff of around 120 firefighters. The service is equipped with 16 heavy appliances (fire tenders, turntable ladders, and specialist four-wheel drive vehicles), four light support vehicles (cars and vans) and four ambulances.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-108">
        <a href="#cite_note-108">
         [108]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Historically, the families of the six ancient parishes of Andorra maintained local arrangements to assist each other in fighting fires. The first fire pump purchased by the government was acquired in 1943. Serious fires which lasted for two days in December 1959 led to calls for a permanent fire service, and the
       <i>
        Andorran Fire Brigade
       </i>
       was formed on 21 April 1961.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-109">
        <a href="#cite_note-109">
         [109]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The fire service maintains full-time cover with five fire crews on duty at any time –  two at the brigade's headquarters in Santa Coloma, and one crew at each of the other three fire stations.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-110">
        <a href="#cite_note-110">
         [110]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Geography">
        Geography
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Andorra&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Geography">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Andorramap.png">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="650" data-file-width="800" height="179" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/Andorramap.png/220px-Andorramap.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/Andorramap.png/330px-Andorramap.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/Andorramap.png/440px-Andorramap.png 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Andorramap.png" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Map of Andorra with its seven parishes labelled
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main articles:
       <a href="/wiki/Geography_of_Andorra" title="Geography of Andorra">
        Geography of Andorra
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Geology_of_Andorra" title="Geology of Andorra">
        Geology of Andorra
       </a>
      </div>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Parishes">
        Parishes
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Andorra&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Parishes">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Parishes_of_Andorra" title="Parishes of Andorra">
        Parishes of Andorra
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       Andorra consists of seven parishes:
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Andorra_la_Vella" title="Andorra la Vella">
         Andorra la Vella
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Canillo" title="Canillo">
         Canillo
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Encamp" title="Encamp">
         Encamp
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Escaldes-Engordany" title="Escaldes-Engordany">
         Escaldes-Engordany
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/La_Massana" title="La Massana">
         La Massana
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Ordino" title="Ordino">
         Ordino
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Sant_Juli%C3%A0_de_L%C3%B2ria" title="Sant Julià de Lòria">
         Sant Julià de Lòria
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_geography">
        Physical geography
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Andorra&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Physical geography">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Grandvalira_ski_resort,_Andorra5.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="768" data-file-width="1024" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Grandvalira_ski_resort%2C_Andorra5.jpg/220px-Grandvalira_ski_resort%2C_Andorra5.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Grandvalira_ski_resort%2C_Andorra5.jpg/330px-Grandvalira_ski_resort%2C_Andorra5.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Grandvalira_ski_resort%2C_Andorra5.jpg/440px-Grandvalira_ski_resort%2C_Andorra5.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Grandvalira_ski_resort,_Andorra5.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Scenery of Andorran mountains
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Andorra_topographic_map-en.svg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1300" data-file-width="1625" height="176" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Andorra_topographic_map-en.svg/220px-Andorra_topographic_map-en.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Andorra_topographic_map-en.svg/330px-Andorra_topographic_map-en.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Andorra_topographic_map-en.svg/440px-Andorra_topographic_map-en.svg.png 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Andorra_topographic_map-en.svg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Topographic map of Andorra
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Due to its location in the eastern
       <a href="/wiki/Pyrenees" title="Pyrenees">
        Pyrenees
       </a>
       mountain range, Andorra consists predominantly of rugged mountains, the highest being the
       <a href="/wiki/Coma_Pedrosa" title="Coma Pedrosa">
        Coma Pedrosa
       </a>
       at 2,942 metres (9,652 ft), and the average elevation of Andorra is 1,996 metres (6,549 ft).
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-111">
        <a href="#cite_note-111">
         [111]
        </a>
       </sup>
       These are dissected by three narrow valleys in a Y shape that combine into one as the main stream, the
       <a href="/wiki/Gran_Valira" title="Gran Valira">
        Gran Valira
       </a>
       river, leaves the country for
       <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">
        Spain
       </a>
       (at Andorra's lowest point of 840 m or 2,756 ft). Andorra's land area is 468 km
       <sup>
        2
       </sup>
       (181 sq mi).
      </p>
      <p>
       <a href="/wiki/Phytogeography" title="Phytogeography">
        Phytogeographically
       </a>
       , Andorra belongs to the Atlantic European province of the
       <a href="/wiki/Circumboreal_Region" title="Circumboreal Region">
        Circumboreal Region
       </a>
       within the
       <a href="/wiki/Boreal_Kingdom" title="Boreal Kingdom">
        Boreal Kingdom
       </a>
       . According to the
       <a href="/wiki/World_Wide_Fund_for_Nature" title="World Wide Fund for Nature">
        WWF
       </a>
       , the territory of Andorra belongs to the
       <a href="/wiki/Ecoregion" title="Ecoregion">
        ecoregion
       </a>
       of Pyrenees conifer and mixed forests.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Climate">
        Climate
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Andorra&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Climate">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Andorra has an
       <a href="/wiki/Alpine_climate" title="Alpine climate">
        alpine climate
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Continental_climate" title="Continental climate">
        continental climate
       </a>
       . Its higher elevation means there is, on average, more snow in winter, lower humidity, and it is slightly cooler in summer.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Economy">
        Economy
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Andorra&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Economy">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Economy_of_Andorra" title="Economy of Andorra">
        Economy of Andorra
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tree_map_export_2009_Andorra.jpeg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="501" data-file-width="640" height="172" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Tree_map_export_2009_Andorra.jpeg/220px-Tree_map_export_2009_Andorra.jpeg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Tree_map_export_2009_Andorra.jpeg/330px-Tree_map_export_2009_Andorra.jpeg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Tree_map_export_2009_Andorra.jpeg/440px-Tree_map_export_2009_Andorra.jpeg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Tree_map_export_2009_Andorra.jpeg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Exports in 2009
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Tourism, the mainstay of Andorra's tiny, well-to-do economy, accounts for roughly 80% of GDP. An estimated 10.2 million tourists visit annually,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-es2_10-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-es2-10">
         [10]
        </a>
       </sup>
       attracted by Andorra's duty-free status and by its summer and winter resorts.
      </p>
      <p>
       One of the main sources of income in Andorra is tourism from ski resorts which total over 175 km (109 mi) of ski ground. The sport brings in over 7 million visitors and an estimated 340 million euros per year, sustaining 2,000 direct and 10,000 indirect jobs at present
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers#Chronological_items" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers">
          <span title="The time period mentioned near this tag is ambiguous. (June 2015)">
           when?
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       The banking sector, with its
       <a href="/wiki/Tax_haven" title="Tax haven">
        tax haven
       </a>
       status, also contributes substantially to the economy (the financial and insurance sector accounts for approximately 19% of GDP
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fs2013_112-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-fs2013-112">
         [112]
        </a>
       </sup>
       ). The financial system comprises five banking groups,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-113">
        <a href="#cite_note-113">
         [113]
        </a>
       </sup>
       one specialised credit entity, 8 investment undertaking management entities, 3 asset management companies and 29 insurance companies, 14 of which are branches of foreign insurance companies authorised to operate in the principality.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fs2013_112-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-fs2013-112">
         [112]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Agricultural production is limited—only 2% of the land is arable—and most food has to be imported. Some tobacco is grown locally. The principal livestock activity is domestic sheep raising. Manufacturing output consists mainly of cigarettes, cigars, and furniture. Andorra's natural resources include hydroelectric power, mineral water, timber, iron ore, and lead.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cia_1-3">
        <a href="#cite_note-cia-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Andorra is not a member of the European Union, but enjoys a
       <a href="/wiki/Andorra%E2%80%93European_Union_relations" title="Andorra–European Union relations">
        special relationship
       </a>
       with it, such as being treated as an EU member for trade in manufactured goods (no tariffs) and as a non-EU member for agricultural products. Andorra lacked a currency of its own and used both the
       <a href="/wiki/French_franc" title="French franc">
        French franc
       </a>
       and the
       <a href="/wiki/Spanish_peseta" title="Spanish peseta">
        Spanish peseta
       </a>
       in banking transactions until 31 December 1999, when both currencies were replaced by the EU's single currency, the euro. Coins and notes of both the franc and the peseta remained legal tender in Andorra until 31 December 2002. Andorra negotiated to issue its own euro coins, beginning in 2014.
      </p>
      <p>
       Andorra has traditionally had one of the world's lowest unemployment rates. In 2009 it stood at 2.9%.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-114">
        <a href="#cite_note-114">
         [114]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Andorra has long benefited from its status as a tax haven, with revenues raised exclusively through import tariffs. However, during the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/European_sovereign-debt_crisis" title="European sovereign-debt crisis">
        European sovereign-debt crisis
       </a>
       of the 21st century, its tourist economy suffered a decline, partly caused by a drop in the prices of goods in
       <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">
        Spain
       </a>
       , which undercut Andorran
       <a href="/wiki/Duty-free_shop" title="Duty-free shop">
        duty-free shopping
       </a>
       . This led to a growth in unemployment. On 1 January 2012, a business tax of 10% was introduced,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-115">
        <a href="#cite_note-115">
         [115]
        </a>
       </sup>
       followed by a
       <a href="/wiki/Sales_tax" title="Sales tax">
        sales tax
       </a>
       of 2% a year later, which raised just over 14 million euros in its first quarter.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116">
        <a href="#cite_note-116">
         [116]
        </a>
       </sup>
       On 31 May 2013, it was announced that Andorra intended to legislate for the introduction of an
       <a href="/wiki/Income_tax" title="Income tax">
        income tax
       </a>
       by the end of June, against a background of increasing dissatisfaction with the existence of tax havens among EU members.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-117">
        <a href="#cite_note-117">
         [117]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The announcement was made following a meeting in Paris between the Head of Government
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Antoni_Marti" title="Antoni Marti">
        Antoni Marti
       </a>
       and the French President and Prince of Andorra,
       <a href="/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Hollande" title="François Hollande">
        François Hollande
       </a>
       . Hollande welcomed the move as part of a process of Andorra "bringing its taxation in line with international standards".
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-118">
        <a href="#cite_note-118">
         [118]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Demographics">
        Demographics
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Andorra&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Demographics">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Andorra_Vall_dels_Cortals_05_JMM.JPG">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2304" data-file-width="3456" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Andorra_Vall_dels_Cortals_05_JMM.JPG/220px-Andorra_Vall_dels_Cortals_05_JMM.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Andorra_Vall_dels_Cortals_05_JMM.JPG/330px-Andorra_Vall_dels_Cortals_05_JMM.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Andorra_Vall_dels_Cortals_05_JMM.JPG/440px-Andorra_Vall_dels_Cortals_05_JMM.JPG 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Andorra_Vall_dels_Cortals_05_JMM.JPG" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         The town of Encamp, Andorra, as seen from the Vall dels Cortals
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Demographics_of_Andorra" title="Demographics of Andorra">
        Demographics of Andorra
       </a>
      </div>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Population">

       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>

         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <table class="toccolours" style="width:15em;border-spacing: 0;float:right;clear:right;margin:0 0 1em 1em;">

      <p>
       The population of Andorra is estimated at 77,281 (2016).
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-UN_WPP_2-2">
        <a href="#cite_note-UN_WPP-2">
         [2]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The population has grown from 5,000 in 1900.
      </p>
      <p>
       Two-thirds of residents lack Andorran nationality and do not have the right to vote in communal elections. Moreover, they are not allowed to be elected as prime minister
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-120">
        <a href="#cite_note-120">
         [120]
        </a>
       </sup>
       or to own more than 33% of the capital stock of a privately held company.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-121">
        <a href="#cite_note-121">
         [121]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-122">
        <a href="#cite_note-122">
         [122]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-123">
        <a href="#cite_note-123">
         [123]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-124">
        <a href="#cite_note-124">
         [124]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Languages">
        Languages
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Andorra&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Languages">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Languages_of_Andorra" title="Languages of Andorra">
        Languages of Andorra
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       The historic and
       <a href="/wiki/Official_language" title="Official language">
        official language
       </a>
       is
       <a href="/wiki/Catalan_language" title="Catalan language">
        Catalan
       </a>
       , a
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Romance_language" title="Romance language">
        Romance language
       </a>
       . The Andorran government encourages the use of Catalan. It funds a Commission for Catalan
       <a href="/wiki/Toponymy" title="Toponymy">
        Toponymy
       </a>
       in Andorra (Catalan:
       <i>
        la Comissió de Toponímia d'Andorra
       </i>
       ), and provides free Catalan classes to assist immigrants. Andorran television and radio stations use Catalan.
      </p>
      <p>
       Because of immigration, historical links, and close geographic proximity,
       <a href="/wiki/Spanish_language" title="Spanish language">
        Spanish
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_language" title="Portuguese language">
        Portuguese
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/French_language" title="French language">
        French
       </a>
       are also commonly spoken. Most Andorran residents can speak one or more of these, in addition to Catalan. English is less commonly spoken among the general population, though it is understood to varying degrees in the major tourist resorts. Andorra is one of only four European countries (together with France, Monaco, and Turkey)
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-125">
        <a href="#cite_note-125">
         [125]
        </a>
       </sup>
       that have never signed the
       <a href="/wiki/Framework_Convention_for_the_Protection_of_National_Minorities" title="Framework Convention for the Protection of National Minorities">
        Council of Europe Framework Convention on National Minorities
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-126">
        <a href="#cite_note-126">
         [126]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       According to the
       <i>
        Observatori Social d'Andorra
       </i>
       , the linguistic usage in Andorra is as follows:
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-127">
        <a href="#cite_note-127">
         [127]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <table border="0" style="border:1px solid #999; background:#fff;">
       <tr style="text-align:center;">
        <th style="background:#ccc;">
         Mother tongue
        </th>
        <th>
         %
        </th>
       </tr>
       <tr style="text-align:center;">
        <td style="background:#ccc;">
         <a href="/wiki/Catalan_language" title="Catalan language">
          Catalan
         </a>
        </td>
        <td>
         38.8%
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr style="text-align:center;">
        <td style="background:#ccc;">
         Spanish
        </td>
        <td>
         35.4%
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr style="text-align:center;">
        <td style="background:#ccc;">
         <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_language" title="Portuguese language">
          Portuguese
         </a>
        </td>
        <td>
         15%
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr style="text-align:center;">
        <td style="background:#ccc;">
         French
        </td>
        <td>
         5.4%
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr style="text-align:center;">
        <td style="background:#ccc;">
         Others
        </td>
        <td>
         5.5%
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr style="text-align:center;">
        <td colspan="2">
         <small>
          <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20130822055051/http://www.iea.ad/images/stories/Documents/CRES/Observatoris/2005/2005_3_PoliticaLinguistica.pdf" rel="nofollow">
           2005 3 PoliticaLinguistica.pdf
          </a>
         </small>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </table>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Religion">
        Religion
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Andorra&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Religion">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The population of Andorra is predominantly (88.2%) Catholic.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-128">
        <a href="#cite_note-128">
         [128]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Their patron saint is
       <a href="/wiki/Our_Lady_of_Meritxell" title="Our Lady of Meritxell">
        Our Lady of Meritxell
       </a>
       . Though it is not an official state religion, the constitution acknowledges a special relationship with the Catholic Church, offering some special privileges to that group
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify">
          <span title="The text near this tag may need clarification or removal of jargon. (August 2014)">
           clarification needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
       . Other Christian denominations include the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Anglican_Church" title="Anglican Church">
        Anglican Church
       </a>
       , the
       <a href="/wiki/Unification_Church" title="Unification Church">
        Unification Church
       </a>
       , the
       <a href="/wiki/New_Apostolic_Church" title="New Apostolic Church">
        New Apostolic Church
       </a>
       , and
       <a href="/wiki/Jehovah%27s_Witnesses" title="Jehovah's Witnesses">
        Jehovah's Witnesses
       </a>
       . The small
       <a href="/wiki/Islam_in_Andorra" title="Islam in Andorra">
        Muslim community
       </a>
       is primarily made up of North African immigrants.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-129">
        <a href="#cite_note-129">
         [129]
        </a>
       </sup>
       There is a small community of
       <a href="/wiki/Hinduism" title="Hinduism">
        Hindus
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Bah%C3%A1%27%C3%AD_Faith_in_Andorra" title="Bahá'í Faith in Andorra">
        Bahá'ís
       </a>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ARDA05_130-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-ARDA05-130">
         [130]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wolfram_131-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Wolfram-131">
         [131]
        </a>
       </sup>
       and roughly 100 Jews live in Andorra.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-132">
        <a href="#cite_note-132">
         [132]
        </a>
       </sup>
       (See
       <a href="/wiki/History_of_the_Jews_in_Andorra" title="History of the Jews in Andorra">
        History of the Jews in Andorra
       </a>
       .)
      </p>
      <h2>
